						OWNER = { is_subject_of = TXS} 
					  }
					}
				  }

		fire_only_once = yes
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
		complete_effect = {
			release = SIC
			SIC = {
				every_core_state = {
					remove_core_of = SIC
				}
			}
			117 = { add_core_of = SIC }
			156 = { add_core_of = SIC }
			1006 = { add_core_of = SIC }
	
			SIC = { 
				every_core_state = {
				  limit = {
					AND = {
					  NOT = { 
						is_core_of = TXS
					  }
					  OR = {
						is_owned_by = TXS
						OWNER = { is_subject_of = TXS} 
					  }
					}
				  }
				  transfer_state_to = SIC
				}
			  }
			SIC = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = TXS_SIC
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus            
	
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Pietro Signorini"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/OIL/Portrait_Cirio_Pietro_Signorini.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = right_technocracy_subtype
				}
				set_popularities = {
					paternal_autocrat = 70
					national_populist = 30
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = "Cirio Directorate"
					long_name = "Cirio Directorate"
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = national_populist
					name = "Cirio Directorate"
					long_name = "Cirio Directorate"
				}
	
				TXS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SIC
						autonomous_state = texas_global_corporate_syndicate
					}
				}
	
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}
	
economy_decisions = {
	TXS_expand_interstate = {
		icon = GFX_decision_road

		allowed = { tag = TXS }

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TXS_improve_inf_I
		}

		cost = 70
		days_remove = 90
		fire_only_once = yes

		modifier = {
			production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.05
			production_speed_infrastructure_factor = 0.2
			production_speed_rail_way_factor = 0.2
		}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 500 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete TXS_expand_interstate"
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove TXS_expand_interstate"
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 375 }
				375 = { add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 instant_build = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 833 }
				833 = { add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 instant_build = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
}
